	GGR_invade_bulgaria = {
		custom_cost_trigger = { always = yes }
		fire_only_once = yes
		visible = {
			NOT = {
				is_in_faction_with = BUL
			}
			country_exists = BUL
			ROM = { exists = no }
		}
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					BUL = {
						is_puppet_of = ITA
					}
					ITA = {
						is_ai = yes
					}
				}
				ITA = { end_puppet = BUL }
				BUL = {
					leave_faction = yes
					load_oob = ITA_BUL_Volenteers
				}
				else = {
					ITA = {
						end_puppet = BUL
					}
					set_global_flag = goring_invading_bul
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						BUL = {
							is_in_faction_with = JAP
						}
						BUL = {
							is_in_faction_with = USA
						}
					}
				}
				BUL = {
					leave_faction = yes
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = BUL
				type = annex_everything
			}
			GER = {
				white_peace = ITA
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = { factor = 20 }
	}

				custom_effect_tooltip = GGR_add_militarist_demands_bad

			else = {
				subtract_from_variable = { GGR_militarist_demands_met = 1 }
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_variable = GGR_militarist_demands_met
					}
				}
				set_variable = { GGR_militarist_demands_met = 2 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = GGR_add_militarist_demands_good
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { GGR_militarist_demands_met = 2 }
			}
			set_variable = { GGR_leaving_militarists = 0 }
		}
	}

	GGR_annex_bohemia = {
		cost = 25
		icon = GFX_decision_ger_reichskommissariats
		fire_only_once = yes

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = GGR_zero_plan
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision GGR_annex_bohemia"
			if = { # Bohemia sided with Göring but died
				limit = {
					CZE = { exists = no }
					has_country_flag = GER_CZE_joined_goring
				}
				country_event = { id = reich.807 days = 3 }
			}
			else_if = { # Bohemia didn't side with Göring
				limit = {
					CZE = { exists = no }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = GER_CZE_joined_goring }
				}
				country_event = { id = reich.806 days = 3 }
			}
			else_if = { # Bohemia sided with Göring and didn't die
				limit = {
					CZE = { exists = yes }
					has_country_flag = GER_CZE_joined_goring
				}
				country_event = { id = reich.809 days = 3 }
			}
			else = { country_event = { id = goering.982 days = 4 } } # Bohemia is neutral
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}

	GGR_invade_ethiopia = {
		cost = 50
		icon = GFX_decision_category_assault
		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_war = yes
			}
		}
		visible = {
			is_in_faction_with = GEA
			OR = {
				country_exists = RPS
				country_exists = SDS
				country_exists = AYA
				country_exists = AZA
				country_exists = ERT
				country_exists = ETB
				country_exists = ORM
				country_exists = KEN
				country_exists = SML
			}
		}
		days_remove = 10
		remove_effect = {
			GGR_increase_militarist_loyalty_large = yes
			GGR_increase_militarist_power_small = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = RPS
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = RPS
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = SDS
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = SDS
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = SDF
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = SDF
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = AZA
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = AZA
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = AYA
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = AYA
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = ERT
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ERT
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = ETB
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ETB
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = ORM
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ORM
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = KEN
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = KEN
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = SML
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = SML
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		cost = 20
		icon = GFX_decision_ger_reichskommissariats

				has_completed_focus = GGR_integration
			}
			check_variable = { GGR_switserland_loot > 0 }
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision GGR_loot_switserland"
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { country_exists = SWI } }
				add_stability = -0.04
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = GGR_integration } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = GGR_integration_stop_chance_switserland
				#custom_effect_tooltip = GGR_loot_player_info

				set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_GDP_boost_flat = GGR_switserland_loot }
				econ_GDP_boost_once_flat = yes
				subtract_from_variable = { GGR_switserland_loot = 2 }
				if = { limit = { check_variable = { GGR_switserland_loot = 0 } }
					clear_variable = GGR_switserland_loot
					custom_effect_tooltip = GGR_loot_runout
				}

				hidden_effect = {
					random_list = {
						45 = {
							set_country_flag = GGR_switserland_unruly
							country_event = { id = goering.829 days = 1 }
						}
						55 = {
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = GGR_not_looting_switserland_tooltip
			}
		}
	}

					econ_GDP_boost_once_flat = yes
					add_stability = -0.03
				}

			set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_GDP_boost_flat = GGR_isles_loot }
			econ_GDP_boost_once_flat = yes

			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GGR_isles_loot = 0 }

			}
		}

ARC_fall_rot_decisions = {
	RUS_send_volunteers= {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_form_nation
		days_re_enable = 10
		fixed_random_seed = no

		visible = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = RUS_all_russian_congress
					event_target:RUS_western_unifier = {
						OR = {
							has_government = ultranationalism
							has_government = esoteric_nazism
						}
					}
					has_government = ultranationalism
					has_government = esoteric_nazism
				}
			}
		}

		available = {
			has_war = no
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_fortifying
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision RUS_send_volunteers"
			set_country_flag = RUS_anti_goering_volunteers
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = no
				}

				if = {
					limit = { has_event_target = RUS_western_unifier }

					set_temp_variable = { target = RUS_western_unifier }
					TNO_increase_volunteer_cap_1 = yes
					custom_effect_tooltip = "TNO_increase_volunteers_western_unifier_1"
				}
				else = {
					set_temp_variable = { target = ONG }
					TNO_increase_volunteer_cap_1 = yes
					custom_effect_tooltip = "TNO_increase_volunteers_ONG_1"
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_event_target = RUS_western_unifier }
					WSR = {
						random_list = {
							70 = {
								load_oob = "ARC_volunteers"
							}
							30 = {
								load_oob = "ARC_volunteers2"
							}
						}
						country_event = { id = ARC.1 }
					}
				}
				else = {
					ONG = {
						random_list = {
							70 = {
								load_oob = "ARC_volunteers"
							}
							30 = {
								load_oob = "ARC_volunteers2"
							}
						}
						country_event = { id = ARC.1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 15
			modifier = {
				add = 8
				WSR = {
					same_government_type_as_ROOT = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 15
				is_neighbor_of = event_target:RUS_western_unifier
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -5
				event_target:RUS_western_unifier = {
					has_government = national_socialism
				}
				NOT = {
					has_government = national_socialism
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -7
				NOT = {
					has_event_target = RUS_western_unifier
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -5
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						event_target:RUS_western_unifier = { original_tag = ROOT }
						event_target:RUS_west_siberia_unifier = { original_tag = ROOT }
						event_target:RUS_central_siberia_unifier = { original_tag = ROOT }
						event_target:RUS_far_east_unifier = { original_tag = ROOT }
						event_target:RUS_kazakhstan_unifier = { original_tag = ROOT }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision GGRCSI_remove_power_focus"

				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GGRCSI_power_for_the_military_sector
				}
				GGRCSI_increase_military_concern = yes
				add_days_remove = { decision = GGRCSI_power_for_the_military_sector days = 2 }
			}
			if = {

					has_country_flag = GGRCSI_power_for_the_civilian_sector
				}
				GGRCSI_increase_public_concern = yes
				add_days_remove = { decision = GGRCSI_power_for_the_civilian_sector days = 2 }
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { GGRCSI_spending = 20 }
			add_to_variable = { GGR_GGRCSI_misc_costs = -0.020 }
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 40
		}
	}

	GGR_invite_iran = {
		cost = 10
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_decision
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_remove = 30

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = GGR_the_southern_route
			OR = {
				country_exists = IRN
				country_exists = PER
			}
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = IRN
					is_in_faction_with = PER
				}
			}
		}

		available = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					country_exists = IRN
					NOT = {
						country_exists = PER
						country_exists = IRI
						country_exists = IRL
						country_exists = IRA
						country_exists = IRB
						country_exists = IRC
					}
				}
				AND = {
					country_exists = PER
					NOT = {
						country_exists = IRN
						country_exists = IRI
						country_exists = IRL
						country_exists = IRA
						country_exists = IRB
						country_exists = IRC
					}
				}
			}
			has_completed_focus = GGR_iranian_military_cooperation
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = GGR_busy_diplomats
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision GGR_invite_iran"
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = IRN
				}
				add_to_faction = IRN
				IRN = {
					econ_join_sphere_GER = yes
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_to_faction = PER
				PER = {
					econ_join_sphere_GER = yes
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = GGR_busy_diplomats
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision GGR_invite_iran_removed"
			remove_ideas = GGR_hostile_iranian_population
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = GGR_iranian_military_cooperation
				}
				add_ideas = GGR_pacified_iranian_population
			}
			clr_country_flag = GGR_busy_diplomats
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 40
		}
	}

					has_war_with = SLG
				}
			}
			GER = {
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = ALG
				}
			}
		}

					country_exists = ILG
				}
				GER = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = ILG
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = SLG
				}
				GER = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = SLG
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = ALG
				}
				GER = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = ALG
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20

				factor = 0
				has_war = yes
			}
		}
	}

	GGR_someone_we_can_actually_work_with = {
		cost = 25
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = GGR_unlock_peter3_decisions
			NOT = {has_country_flag = GGR_serbwar}

		}

		available = {
			GGR_not_invaded_serbia = yes
			has_political_power > 24
			NOT = {has_country_flag = GGR_serbwar}
		}
		fire_only_once = yes

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = GGR_serbpeace
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision GGR_someone_we_can_actually_work_with"
			set_variable = { GGR_chetnik_diplomacy = 0 }
			set_variable = { GGR_chetnik_integration = 0 }

			if = {
				limit = {
					HUN = {
						OR = {
							exists = no
							is_subject_of = GER
						}
					}
					CRO = {
						OR = {
							exists = no
							is_subject_of = GER
						}
					}
				}
				set_variable = { GGR_chetnik_diplomacy_target = 0 }
				set_variable = { GGR_chetnik_integration_target = 1.99 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					CRO = {
						OR = {
							exists = no
							is_subject_of = GER
						}
					}
				}
				set_variable = { GGR_chetnik_diplomacy_target = 1.99 }
				set_variable = { GGR_chetnik_integration_target = 0.99 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					HUN = {
						OR = {
							exists = no
							is_subject_of = GER
						}
					}
				}
				set_variable = { GGR_chetnik_diplomacy_target = 0.99 }
				set_variable = { GGR_chetnik_integration_target = 1.99 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					CRO = {
						is_in_faction_with = GER
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Jure Francetić"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
				}
				set_variable = { GGR_chetnik_diplomacy_target = 3.99 }
				set_variable = { GGR_chetnik_integration_target = 0.99 }
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { GGR_chetnik_diplomacy_target = 2.99 }
				set_variable = { GGR_chetnik_integration_target = 0 }
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
		}
	}
